Japan Notifies Withdrawal From the London Naval Conference Japanese Representative Formally Announces at Today's Meeting Britain, the United States, France, and Italy Decide to Continue Holding Four-Nation Conference

London It was formally announced here today that Japan has withdrawn from the London Naval Conference. The announcement was made after the Naval Conference decided to adjourn until 3:00 pm on Wednesday to allow the Japanese representative to consult Tokyo. (National Telegram on the 13th)

London It is reported that the Japanese delegation to the Naval Conference has notified the delegations of Britain, the United States, France, and Italy of its intention to withdraw from the conference. The General Committee will meet tomorrow, at which time the Japanese delegation will formally announce its withdrawal and explain the reasons. According to this reporter's knowledge, after Japan withdraws from the Naval Conference, the delegations of Britain, the United States, France, and Italy will continue negotiations. (Havas dispatch on the 14th)

London It is reported that Japanese representatives Nagano and Nagai met with Foreign Secretary Eden, Naval Secretary Monsell, Chief of Naval Operations Chatfield, and Counselor Daleyki at the British Admiralty at 6:10 pm on the 13th and discussed the procedures of the First Committee meeting for two hours. As a result, there is no hope for the establishment of the common maximum proposal of the Japanese government. Therefore, the Japanese delegation sent a letter to the British delegation on the evening of the 13th, formally notifying that the Japanese representatives would not attend the meeting in the future. The content is that the Nagano plenipotentiary will attend the First Committee at 3:00 pm on the 15th to explain the Japanese government's proposal but will not request that the proposal be put to a vote. After the adjournment of the First Committee on the 15th, the Japanese representatives will not attend the meeting. Although the four countries of the United States, France, Italy, and Britain will continue to discuss, Japan will not participate in this discussion. (Domei dispatch on the 13th)

London British naval experts today predicted that Japan's withdrawal from the London Naval Conference will have the following effects: Japan's position in East Asia will become more consolidated, and it can step up its plan to dominate China. The Anglo-Japanese understanding movement on mutual interests in China will tend to stall. Britain will seek the understanding of the United States and will seek an understanding on the East and the Pacific. It is said that Britain hopes that the United States will help it sanction Japan's expansion plan. The dictatorship of the Japanese warlords will become more profound, and popular groups that support parliamentary politics will return to the dark ages as after the Manchurian Incident from 1931 to 1932. (National Telegram on the 14th)

Situation at Today's Meeting Five Countries Will Declare No Competition in Shipbuilding

London Whether Japan will continue to participate in the Naval Conference is still a question today. This depends on how the chairman can safely navigate the difficult issue of Japan's equality demands at the next meeting of the First Committee, because the outcome of the vote on this issue will inevitably cause Japan to leave the conference. Although the attitude of the Japanese delegation makes people firmly believe that the dispute over equality demands must be dealt with sooner or later, there was an unexpected development in the conference affairs last night, because after the British and Japanese delegations met for two hours, it was announced that today's important meeting would be postponed again to allow the Japanese representatives to continue to ask Tokyo for instructions. According to news here today, if Japan withdraws from the conference, it intends to suggest that the five countries issue a joint declaration stating that they do not want to compete in shipbuilding, so that the friendly relations between the countries will not be disturbed. News from Tokyo said that if the Naval Conference causes an arms race due to the postponement, Japan intends to try to adjust international relations. All newspapers here said that if Japan's equality proposal is put to a vote, it will inevitably be rejected. If so, Japan will definitely stop participating in the Naval Conference. However, all newspapers expect that other countries will not hastily put Japan's proposal to a vote. The conference will agree to accept this proposal and continue to study it, so that the five-nation conference can safely proceed with the issue of qualitative restrictions. (Reuters dispatch on the 14th)

London According to the Naval Conference's reporter, the Japanese delegation will withdraw from the conference after the General Committee meets in the next two days. Although this is not the final decision in theory, there is no major change. The result of the consultations between the British and Japanese delegations yesterday has proved that there is absolutely no possibility of a compromise on Japan's proposal for a common maximum amount of naval power. According to British representatives, the country was originally prepared to further discuss Japan's demands, but when Britain consulted with other delegations, all of them opposed the Japanese proposal, showing that a compromise was indeed hopeless. When the General Committee meets tomorrow, all of its time will be spent listening to the report of the Japanese representatives and the replies that the representatives of other countries intend to propose. However, it is expected that the report of the Japanese representatives will be very lengthy, so the replies of the representatives of various countries will largely be postponed to the meeting the day after tomorrow. According to this reporter, the wording of the Japanese representatives' report is still mild. The purpose of this is probably not to allow the countries to use Japan's tough attitude as an excuse to blame Japan for the failure of the Naval Conference. Generally speaking, the Naval Conference will end in the middle of this week, unless a miracle occurs that can suddenly change Japan's attitude, then there is no hope of reversing the country's withdrawal, because the country's delegation has asked Tokyo for instructions on the procedures to be taken when withdrawing from the conference. As far as the representatives of other countries are concerned, the representatives of Britain and the United States met once this morning and contacted the representatives of France and Italy separately beforehand. As a result, it is heard that it has been decided that after Japan withdraws from the conference, the representatives of the four countries will continue to meet. At that time, it will be difficult to understand whether Japan will send observers to attend to monitor the development of the conference. Regarding this level, the Japanese delegation declared that the country's attitude will be based on the positions taken by the representatives of other countries at the meetings in the next two days. (Havas dispatch on the 14th)

Tokyo The Japanese government, due to the fact that the disarmament conference has reached a state of actual breakup, is preparing to declare Japan's disarmament policy to China and foreign countries, and to notify the people of the international situation after the breakup. At the same time, it is studying Pacific defense and other necessary issues with related agencies such as the Army and Navy. (Domei Telegram on the 14th)

Movements in Japanese Industry: Naval Competition Benefits Industry

Tokyo: At the International Disarmament Conference convened in London, Japan's proposed common maximum limit was not approved. Consequently, the Japanese plenipotentiary announced their withdrawal from the Disarmament Conference. Regarding this matter, concerning the impact on Japanese industry, the views of the industrial sector are summarized as follows: The breakdown of the Disarmament Conference was largely anticipated. Contingency measures were already considered and incorporated during the compilation of this year's military budget. Now that the breakdown of the conference is a reality, although countries may not immediately engage in competitive shipbuilding, it is self-evident that this will ignite their military expansion fervor. From a domestic perspective, this will be influenced by the current improvement in the British and American financial sectors, and thus the Japanese domestic industrial sector will also take advantage of the momentum to prosper. However, in the future, the military-related industries of the United Kingdom and the United States will experience greater development, leading to better financial conditions, and the Japanese financial sector will also benefit from this. As for domestic military-related industries such as ironworks, shipbuilding, and chemical industries, they will continue to exhibit vitality. As a result, the entire industrial sector can develop an active situation. From an external perspective, export trade will not suffer a blow in the future and will continue to maintain last year's advantages. The instability of the European political situation and the atmosphere will become increasingly perilous. The international relations between Britain, France, Italy, and Germany cannot be resolved quickly. Ultimately, Japan seems to have considerable benefits to gain. Furthermore, with the continued improvement of the British and American financial sectors, Japanese goods can also be exported more to Europe and the United States. As for the Far East, Near East, and Southeast Asia, Japanese goods are traditionally recognized for their low prices and good quality. Now, due to the renewed recognition of Japan's national strength, an increase in exports can also be expected. In the past, the export of Japanese goods has overcome countless obstacles to achieve today's prosperity. Therefore, even if more obstacles arise in the future, it will surely proceed smoothly and will not lead to pessimistic situations. As for the China issue, Japan should strive to promote the normalization of Sino-Japanese relations from its own independent position. China will also correct its perceptions based on the global situation. Therefore, in this aspect, we believe that improvement can be expected. It seems that observation is not without possibility, and so on. (14th Associated Press dispatch)

British-Egyptian Relations; Lampson Stresses the Necessity of a Military Alliance

Cairo: Sir Miles Lampson, the British High Commissioner in Egypt, met today with Pasha, the leader of the Egyptian "United Front" political party, and announced Britain's views on the Egyptian political situation, especially regarding the request for a British-Egyptian agreement based on the 1930 treaty. Sir Miles Lampson strongly argued that Egypt's military status had undergone major changes since 1930. For example, the 1930 treaty stipulated that 8,000 British troops be transported to the Suez Canal, but since then, the western part of Egypt has become a very important military location, and it takes considerable time to transport troops from the Suez Canal to the west. Finally, Sir Miles said that an Egyptian-British military alliance is very important, but Britain must know the attitude of Egyptian leaders on various public issues. At the same time, British military preparations are very rapid, and 5,000 sailors have set sail for Egypt. The current number of British troops stationed in Egypt is 40,000, and all kinds of military supplies, firearms, etc., continue to arrive in Egypt. Bolivian-Paraguayan Peace Draft; Contains Four Recommendations

Washington: After several months of work, the Chaco Peace Conference has drafted a peace agreement between Paraguay and Bolivia, containing four recommendations: The two countries exchange prisoners of war. Bolivia pays a certain amount of money as nominal compensation for Paraguay's losses in the war. The two countries restore diplomatic relations. An unarmed zone is demarcated in the Chaco region, and each neutral country sends a committee to reside there to ensure Paraguay's security. The above draft has been agreed upon by the delegations of both Paraguay and Bolivia to the Peace Conference and is now being studied by the two governments. A copy has recently been sent to the US State Department. (13th Havas dispatch)

Italy; Women's Patriotic Spirit; Adopting Domestic Goods

Recently, the National Clothing Bureau, in order to encourage the use of domestic goods, specially created a special mark. All women's skirts made of domestic materials and using domestic styles must wear them for identification. The National Clothing Bureau's move is intended to stimulate the patriotic spirit of women. (13th Havas dispatch)

Pittman; Observations on Silver; US Silver Purchase Act Continues to Exist; Expects China and Mexico to Restore Silver Standard

Washington: Senate silver advocate Pittman stated today that the US Silver Purchase Act of 1934 will remain in effect, although some leading merchants have proposed repealing or amending the Act. Pittman also criticized the annual report released yesterday by Handy & Harman, saying, "I greatly admire the company's observation of silver from a commodity perspective, but their observation of silver is only that. I am different. I always consider silver from a currency perspective and use this as a starting point." Pittman criticized foreign governments for using propaganda and other methods to oppose the US silver law and predicted that China, Mexico, and other countries will soon restore the silver standard or expand the use of silver. Senate inflation advocate Thomas stated that Handy & Harman's opposition to the silver law is due to the fact that the company's business and commissions have suffered losses after the implementation of the law. Before the United States purchased silver from foreign countries, the company actually manipulated the price of silver in the United States and earned commissions from it. Since the United States began purchasing silver from Mexico, Peru, Chile, and other places, the company's business has plummeted. Frankly speaking, the entire silver plan is manipulated by the enemy. Thomas stated after meeting with Mexican economic expert Oruza that he knew Mexico expressed good feelings about the plan, but it is difficult to say what will happen in the future. (13th National Agency dispatch)

China's Monetary Policy Successful; 100 Million Ounces of Silver Sold to US

London: According to news from New York, the US government plans to purchase 500 million ounces of silver from China, and 100 million ounces have already been transacted. The Financial Times recently stated that if this is true, China can earn 300 million US dollars from the price of silver, which is enough to support the new monetary policy recently implemented by the Chinese government. According to news received here, the Chinese government's efforts to stabilize the country's currency price have been satisfactory to date. (13th Havas dispatch)

US Supreme Court Ruling; Government Loses Again; Loses 200 Million Gold in Agricultural Products Sales Tax; Government Advantageous in Pennhyd Case Appeal Dismissed

Washington: The US Supreme Court, which convened for only ten minutes today, has already caused the government to lose US$200 million in agricultural products sales tax, and the fate of another US$1 billion in collected sales tax remains uncertain. Regarding the Pennhyd Cotton Production Control Act, no direct ruling was made. According to the agricultural products sales tax portion, the appellants were eight rice mills in Louisiana. The Supreme Court ruled that all taxes paid during the litigation period must be refunded. As for other paid sales taxes, merchants must prove that they have not recovered this tax from consumers before they can demand a refund. Therefore, the future of the US$1 billion already collected by the government is still difficult to determine. The court dismissed the lawsuit of appellant Moore regarding the Pennhyd Cotton Production Control Act due to legal procedural reasons. However, the government of the state of Georgia also has a lawsuit regarding this Act on January 20, so it is still to be ruled at that time. (13th National Telegram)

Washington: The United States Supreme Court today ruled on two cases related to President Roosevelt's New Deal measures, one favorable to the government and one unfavorable to the government. The court upheld the Pennhyd Cotton Management Act and canceled the case of Moore in Texas, but in the case of the Louisiana rice mill, the court announced a ruling unfavorable to the government. Although the Pennhyd case is related to the New Deal measures, it is the work of the senators of the cotton-producing states, not the government itself. As for the Louisiana case, the court believes that the 200 million fee donation must be returned to the manufacturers. The court currently does not want to express its opinion on whether the Pennhyd case is legal or not, so its ruling can be considered favorable to the government. However, another lawsuit filed by the Governor of Georgia will give the Supreme Court the opportunity to continue to adjudicate the Pennhyd case. Pennhyd now claims that the bill he initiated is now effective and the Department of Agriculture has the right to continue to handle it in accordance with it to relieve cotton farmers. Cotton production this year can be protected. The reason why the Supreme Court justices did not express their views on the legality of the Pennhyd case is because they believe that this is a matter that should be tried by the lower courts and should not be brought before the Supreme Court. Therefore, the cancellation of this appeal cannot be regarded as a legal judgment of this case, and the fee donation that has already been paid to the cotton farmers can be recovered by the taxpayers. This is still an undecided issue, so the government's fear caused by the cancellation of the Agricultural Adjustment Act has not diminished.

The Louisiana rice mill case was filed by several rice mills in the state, requesting that the government be prevented from collecting fee donations based on the reason that this is not a true donation tax. The rice mill argued that this kind of donation tax is one of the ways to manage agricultural products. The government abused the collection of donation taxes, and therefore, it can only be used to raise national income to seek the well-being of the whole, rather than to seek the interests of a part of the people. (13th Reuters dispatch)

Washington: The Supreme Court's order yesterday that the government return the 200 million yuan it collected in fee donations to the Louisiana rice mills has caused the government to have an income and expenditure of 1 billion yuan. The Agricultural Adjustment Act has been revised, stipulating that if the Agricultural Adjustment Act is illegal, the donor can claim it back from the government. The fee donation is only part of what they pay from ordinary interests and has not been transferred to consumers. Now the Agricultural Adjustment Act has indeed been judged to be illegal, but this amendment has not yet been declared invalid by the court, so it depends on how the court rules whether the government will pay back 100 million yuan. In addition, there is still one point between the Supreme Court and the government, which is the Pennhyd Act. Although the court refused to accept the lawsuit filed by the cotton planters in Texas against this bill yesterday, it did not express the opinion that this bill is legal. The public believes that the lawsuit filed by the Governor of Georgia will inevitably fail the Pennhyd case when it is heard in the future. If the government cannot find an alternative solution, the failure of the Pennhyd Act will inevitably have a major impact on world cotton prices. (14th Reuters dispatch)

New Soil Conservation Plan; Replaces the Agricultural Adjustment Act; Principles Approved by the National Farmers Union

Washington: The government's new soil conservation plan, which is used to replace the Agricultural Adjustment Act, has been approved in principle today by the executive meeting of the American General Farmers Union. The Association declared that the Soil Conservation Program has clearly completed a satisfactory plan for agricultural control. However, the Association requested that the government not repeal the law to deposit 30 percent of tariffs to subsidize agricultural exports. This plan is also named the Export Subsidy Program, which has been rejected by government leaders. President Roosevelt recently specifically raised the case to the press, considering it to be out of date. (13th National Telegram)

Mayors Request Allocation; Relief for 800,000 Unemployed

Washington: Mayors of major US cities today requested Congress to allocate $2,340,000,000 to continue federal relief work until July 1, 1937. The mayors' requirements were directly submitted to Vice President Garner and House Speaker Byrns. The main purpose of this proposal, according to the mayors, is that the new work relief program led by Hopkins has failed to provide jobs for the 800,000 people awaiting relief. Local governments are now facing a serious problem, as they must take care of the food and clothing of those who have not obtained work. (13th National Telegram)

Famous British Writer Rudyard Kipling Critically Ill; His Works Popular Worldwide, Royalties Exceed £350,000

London—Famous author Rudyard Kipling is seriously ill. After undergoing surgery at the Middlesex Hospital yesterday morning, his condition is now critical. It is reported that he is suffering from a severe stomach ailment. Kipling, aged 70, left his home in Sussex last week and arrived in London to prepare for a winter trip abroad, as he often travels when feeling unwell. The hospital issued a report last night stating that Mr. Kipling's condition was quite serious, but he was still able to hold on a month ago. Another report issued early this morning stated that his condition was very critical at midnight. Kipling is married to an American woman, and his works are beloved by Americans. According to his publisher, Doubleday, Doran & Company, Kipling's works sell 100,000 copies annually without slowing down. In the past forty years, his works have sold 3.5 million copies in the United States, with royalties exceeding $1.75 million (or £350,000). The most popular work is "The Jungle Book," which has sold 250,000 copies in the United States since its publication in 1894. Last year, Doubleday, Doran & Company published a selection of Kipling's essays and poems titled "The Kipling Pageant" in commemoration of Kipling's December 30th birthday. The American Literary Guild selected it as a featured publication for December, and over 100,000 copies were sold in the first month. (Reuters Dispatch, 14th)

National Language Lecture: How to Read (Part 2)

Xia Gaizun, Chief Editor of Guanming Bookstore

The above is about reference books. Because the topic of reference books is determined at any time, when reading reference books, you must pay attention to the topic you are referring to, and don't let the topic be wasted. You should also pay attention to the preface and table of contents of that book, remember the general situation, and prepare for future convenient flipping.

The following should be about books for cultivating interest. I have talked about this type of book last time. The number does not need to be large, and the selection should be precise. You can just read one type of book until you are tired. This type of book should also make full use of reference books. For example, if you are now reading Du Fu's poetry collection, then sometimes you have to flip through Du Fu's biography, as well as other people's poetry talks about Du Fu's comments, and so on. If you are reading Wang Yangming's "Instructions for Practical Living," you have to flip through Wang Yangming's collection of works, his biographies, and the works of later generations on the debates between Cheng-Zhu and Lu-Wang schools. Make the book you are reading the center, and then use other books to help, so that you can make the book you are reading more clear, more practical, and more flavorful, and avoid the problem of superficiality.

The above is about the reading methods of three types of books. Regarding the word "reading" itself, there are still a few points I want to talk about. I just divided textbooks into two types of nature, one belongs to general science, which has a strict system, and one belongs to language and writing, which does not have a strict system. I also said that those belonging to general science should focus on reading, and those belonging to language and writing are not enough to just read, and should focus on reciting. Now let me go further, all books are written in language and writing. According to the general situation, a book can contain two kinds of nature. The book itself has content, and there is a system to be found in the content, and the nature belongs to general science. The book is written in language and writing, and if you study it from the form, it belongs to language and writing. A "Historical Records," from its content, is history, but you can also choose an article to use as a national language teaching material. The math textbooks you use, of course, belong to the math category, but from the perspective of language and writing, it is not impossible to use it as a writing reference model. The articles in math books are simple, accurate, and the order is very complete. It is a good example of academic writing. In this way, any book can be said in two ways. If you only look at the content, you can just read it. If you regard it as language and writing, then you must read it.

This broadcast, the Ministry of Education asked me to be responsible for the middle school national language lecture. I limit my lecture to reading, and what I talk about is only the general reading situation, and I have not specifically talked about the national language subject. You may say that what I said does not meet the scope and conditions set by the Ministry of Education. I have to declare that I do not recognize many independent so-called national language books. Among books, except for a very small number of grammar and rhetoric categories, everything else may not belong to the national language subject. Can we say that "The Analects," "Mencius," "Zhuangzi," and "Zuo Zhuan" are national language? Can we say that "Dream of the Red Chamber," "Water Margin," and "Romance of the Three Kingdoms" are national language? But if you focus on the form and study it as language and writing, then there is nothing that is not material for the national language subject. Not only "The Analects," "Mencius," "Zhuangzi," and "Zuo Zhuan" are national language, "Dream of the Red Chamber," "Water Margin," and "Romance of the Three Kingdoms" are national language, but also your physics textbooks and botany textbooks are national language, even Zhang San's land deed and Li Si's family letter are also national language. I think the so-called national language subject is a kind of homework for learning language and writing. Taking things that were originally written in language and writing and studying them as language and writing is the task of the national language subject. That's why I only talk about general reading and don't specifically bring up the national language subject. Please pay attention to this point.

Studying any book from the perspective of language and writing can be said to belong to the work of the national language subject. Reading can usually be divided into two types: skimming and intensive reading. The purpose of skimming is to understand and obtain content, and the purpose of intensive reading is to figure out and appreciate. I think that if you want to study the rules of language and writing, you should focus on intensive reading. The amount does not need to be large, but you must read carefully. It's like copying a calligraphy model. The purpose of copying a certain model is to match the brush strokes and write the character with its spirit, not to copy its words. Assuming that this model has a total of one thousand characters, instead of blindly copying it and writing one or two characters for the whole thing, it is better to select ten or twenty characters with changes and interesting meanings, and practice each character carefully several times, which will be more effective. When you read a novel, assuming it is Mao Dun's "Midnight," if you are learning language and writing, you should not pay attention to the story in the book, but you should pay close attention to the character descriptions, narrative methods, structure, and wording and sentence construction in the book. When you read poetry, assuming it is Xu Zhimo's poetry collection, if you are learning language and writing, you should not only pay attention to the general meaning of the poem, but also pay attention to its sentence construction, rhyme, rhythm, and aspects of expression, imagination, antithesis, and style. The changes and techniques in language and writing are actually not very many. As long as you can pay attention, you can probably see it in a small part. Assuming a book has five hundred pages, and each page has one thousand words, if you can understand the first page, then I dare to guarantee that you can understand the whole book. Because all the rules of language and writing in the whole book have probably appeared in the first page of one thousand words. For example, grammatical rules, such as the use of verbs, the use of conjunctions, the use of adjectives, the use of auxiliary words, and the combination of various sentences, have all appeared on the first page. I advise you to put more effort into intensive reading.

Due to time constraints, my words are about to end. I feel that there are many messy and incomplete places in what I have said. Please ask your teachers to correct them for me. Regarding reading in the middle school national language subject, I published many opinions a few years ago. What I said is quite different from this time. I remember there are two articles, one is called "On the Learning of Chinese Language," which is published in the "Learning Methods of Various Subjects in Middle School" in the Kaiming Youth Series, and the other is called "What Should Be Read Outside of Chinese Language Class," which is published in the "Art of Reading" in the Middle School Student Magazine. If you have never seen them, please go and see them yourself, or you may get some supplements for my lecture this time. My boring lecture wasted your after-school time. I'm very sorry. (End)

Sino-British Yunnan-Burma Boundary Demarcation Commissioners Arrive at Survey Site

The Sino-British Yunnan-Burma boundary demarcation commissioners and all staff arrived at the survey site of the undefined section of Yunnan-Burma boundary on the afternoon of November 30. The British side was stationed in Hu Suan, and the Chinese side was stationed in Nan Da, three miles east of Hu Suan. At 10:30 a.m. on December 1, the British commissioner welcomed the Chinese commissioner half a mile away from Hu Suan. At 11:00 a.m., the Chinese commissioner, along with Chief Secretary Mr. Li and 200 guards, arrived in Hu Suan by car. The British army gave a rifle salute to pay tribute. They invited the Chinese commissioner into the tent for tea and snacks. At 1:00 p.m., the Chinese and British commissioners jointly welcomed Mr. Islyn, a neutral commissioner specially appointed by the League of Nations. The national flags of China and Britain were raised in Hu Suan, and each side sent four soldiers to guard them. Other troops were lined up on the left and right. When the neutral commissioner Islyn arrived in Hu Suan, the Chinese army sounded the horn to welcome him. At the same time, the British army gave a rifle salute to pay tribute. Neutral Commissioner Islyn returned the salute to express his thanks. After the ceremony, he entered the tent prepared by the British side and opened a welcome meeting. British Commissioner Gross gave a speech, saying that he hoped that both parties would embrace the spirit of mutual concession in this demarcation to achieve the goal of success. Chinese Commissioner Liang Yugao said that he trusted that Britain was the most just country in the world and would never treat China unfairly. Neutral Commissioner Islyn said that he hoped that the Sino-British parties would not need him to say a word to demarcate the boundary, and so on. After that, the British side provided lunch, and the meeting ended.

Catastrophic Flood in Ten Counties of Western Shandong to Cause Losses Reaching 100 Million Yuan, Local Vitality Unlikely to Recover Within a Decade

Jinan Correspondence: The unprecedented flood in western Shandong last year, after a thorough investigation and statistics of the disaster losses by the Commissioner's Office of the Experimental Zone, is truly alarming. The hardest-hit areas include over 300 villages around Wang Guitun in the southwest of Jinning, over 300 villages in the south of Yuncheng, over 300 villages north of Qili River in Heze, over 600 villages north of Juye city, over 500 villages around Makeng in Yutai, over 300 villages in the southwest of Dongping, over 100 villages in Menguanji, Wenshang, over 60 villages in the northeast of Jinxiang, over 200 villages between the Zhao Wang and Zhu Rivers in Jiaxiang, and over 400 villages south of the dike in Juancheng. Currently, as the breaches have not been closed, the plains are still flooded to a depth of three to four feet, houses have collapsed, and livestock have been washed away. Apart from deaths, many disaster victims have fled to various counties. Even if they return to their villages, they not only lack clothing and food, but also have no land to cultivate and no houses to live in. Seeds, farm tools, cattle, and horses are all missing, and their livelihoods have been cut off, urgently requiring assistance. According to the statistics of the Commissioner's Office, the total property loss in these ten counties amounts to 97,888,000 yuan, truly an unprecedented catastrophe. Scientific Miscellany

— Edited by the Science Society of China

Artificial Silk - Gao Fei

Looking at the name "artificial silk," we know that it is not silk spun by silkworms but a product created by scientists using synthetic methods. Although this invention has only been around for over fifty years, it now occupies a vast market in the world and has become one of the main fabrics welcomed by people. If we happily go to a silk store and look around, what is displayed in the glass windows and piled on the counters—shiny yarn, Parisian silk... all kinds of colors, a dazzling array—all of this is just artificial silk, or fabrics made by randomly combining artificial silk with silk, cotton, wool, etc.

Raw Materials for Artificial Silk Although there are many types of fabrics woven from artificial silk, the raw material is only one type: plant cellulose. Cellulose is a carbohydrate, which is the main component of all plants. However, since there are too many types of plants in the world, the amount of cellulose contained in plants varies. Cotton has the highest cellulose content, containing as much as 90%, while ramie also contains 80%. As for rice straw, bamboo, and wood, they only contain about 50%.

The Invention of Artificial Silk The first person to invent artificial silk was Count de Chardonnet of France in 1885. He dissolved cellulose in nitric acid to make low-nitrated cellulose, which is guncotton and can be used to make smokeless gunpowder. Then, he dissolved the nitrated cellulose in a mixture of alcohol and ether while hot to form a viscous substance. Then, he applied a pressure of 50 atmospheres to extrude this viscous substance through fine holes with a diameter of 0.08mm. Although the extruded material solidifies on the outside, it still retains the viscous substance inside. Taking advantage of this, very fine artificial silk can be made from it. However, since the silk contains nitric acid, it is easy to catch fire. To remove this weakness, after the alcohol and ether mixture has evaporated, ammonium sulfide must be used to completely wash away the nitric acid.

Types of Artificial Silk Production The raw material for artificial silk—cellulose—is truly an inexhaustible resource on the earth. However, dissolving it is not an easy task. Except for dissolving it with strong acid or strong alkali solutions, all other solutions are useless. Because of the different types of solutions used, the production of artificial silk is divided into four types. The following is a summary of these four types:

Nitrated Cellulose Artificial Silk Same as the invention of artificial silk, omitted.

Cuprammonium Hydroxide Solution Cellulose Artificial Silk The first step is to prepare the cuprammonium hydroxide solution. The method is to add caustic soda to copper sulfate solution, which will produce a precipitate. Then, add this precipitate to ammonia solution to obtain a dark blue cuprammonium hydroxide solution. The second step is to soak the cellulose in caustic soda solution for ten minutes, take it out, wash it with water, and then dissolve it in the prepared cuprammonium hydroxide solution to become acidified cuprammonium cellulose. Then, extrude this acidified cuprammonium cellulose solution through fine holes into sulfuric acid, which will solidify it into beautiful and shiny silk.

Viscose Artificial Silk Treat wood pulp for papermaking with caustic soda, then dissolve it in carbon disulfide to obtain a strongly viscous, orange-yellow solution. This solution can be used to manufacture photographic film, electrical insulators, artificial ivory, waterproof cloth, etc. As for the method of making artificial silk, this solution is also extruded through fine holes into ammonium chloride or sulfuric acid, and the sulfide is washed away to obtain solid and high-quality silk.

Cellulose Acetate Artificial Silk Add cotton or wood pulp to a mixed solution of glacial acetic acid, dehydrating acetic acid, and concentrated sulfuric acid, which will dissolve it to obtain cellulose acetate. In addition to dissolving cellulose acetate in acetone, chloroform, glacial acetic acid, etc., and extruding it through fine holes into water to make artificial silk, this material can also be used to manufacture photographic film, electrical insulators, and coatings for aircraft wings. Because this material only burns at the point of contact with fire and does not spread to other parts, it has the advantage.

Because there are the above four different manufacturing methods, each type of artificial silk produced has its own different characteristics. Although the raw materials are abundant and cheap, if the consumption of raw material treatment, the length of manufacturing time, and labor costs are taken into account, the value of artificial silk fabrics on the market will vary accordingly due to these differences.

The Relationship between Artificial Silk and Coal Tar Dyes Coal tar is the black, oily liquid with an unpleasant odor produced after the dry distillation of coal. This liquid was considered waste a hundred years ago, but now it has become an important raw material in industry. In addition to extracting many different important oils from this liquid, it can also be used to synthesize many dyes. The first person to invent the use of this liquid to synthesize dyes was Perpin of England in 1856, who obtained mauvine from the oxidation of aniline, as well as magenta and methyl violet dyes. Since then, many researchers have emerged, and today, the more than ten thousand synthetic dyes sold on the market are all thanks to coal tar, which was previously considered waste. The application of science is about how to turn what the general public considers waste into something useful for the masses. This is what scientists consider a major effort. From this, we can better understand how close and important science is to human life. I've gone too far. Now, let's get back to the topic. What is the use of dyes? The use of dyes is to dye fabrics made of cotton, hemp, wool, and silk in various colors. However, the essence of cotton and hemp is cellulose, while the essence of wool and silk is protein. Protein is easy to dye, while cellulose is more difficult. We can dye fabrics made of a single raw material, or we can dye fabrics made of artificial silk, cotton, hemp, wool, and silk in any combination. Therefore, if we look at fabrics made of any combination before dyeing, they initially look very white and even. However, after dyeing, each type of thread absorbs a special dye, and the complex composition is revealed as desired. The colors are soft, elegant, bright, and colorful, making the world more bright and joyful. Artificial silk increases its beauty because of dyes, and dyes expand their use because of artificial silk. They can truly be called inseparable brothers, complementing each other.

Comparison of Artificial Silk and Silk in Various Aspects Since the advent of artificial silk, its production volume has been increasing rapidly year by year, its quality has been improving day by day, and its demand has been expanding day by day, thus forming the only strong competitor to silk. The world's silk market has almost been monopolized by artificial silk. Here is a comparison of silk and artificial silk in various aspects, from which we can see that the future of artificial silk is booming and unlimited:

Quality As mentioned above, the essence of artificial silk is composed of cellulose, while the essence of silk is composed of protein. Although there are small differences in essence, due to the gradual improvement and increasing perfection of artificial silk, there are no difficulties in its application. Here are the three main points where the quality of artificial silk is currently inferior to that of silk, listed for comparison: First, artificial silk is heavier than silk, so the fabrics woven from it are also heavier and not as light as silk. Second, the elasticity of artificial silk is lower than that of silk, so the woven fabrics do not easily return to their original state after being wrinkled, which detracts from their appearance. Third, the strength of artificial silk is only one-third of that of silk and it easily absorbs moisture. In addition, the luster, dyeing, and weave of artificial silk are completely comparable to those of silk. As for our ability to freely customize any form we need—long or short, thick or thin, flat or round, shiny or matte—artificial silk can fully adapt, and a single strand can be spun into thousands of yards long without any knots or breaks, which is worthy of our admiration.

Weave The essence of artificial silk is not as good as that of silk, but in terms of fabric suitability, it is not only comparable to silk, but also has two points that silk cannot match. Artificial silk can also be proud of this: First, artificial silk is suitable for weaving thick silk. Second, artificial silk has special applicability for wide fabrics, allowing it to be interwoven with wool and cotton.

Price The price of artificial silk has been falling in the market in recent years, just like silk. On the surface, it seems to be a bad phenomenon, but if we actually investigate, we should only worry about silk and not about artificial silk! In the last twenty years, the production of silk has not even doubled, while the increase in artificial silk has been more than twenty-two times. The price of artificial silk has fallen only because it is mechanically produced, and the cost can be quickly reduced due to technological improvements and the needs of society, resulting in increased production efficiency. Silk is different. The price of silk has fallen entirely because the market has been taken over, and it has no choice but to do so. Because silk is a type of agriculture and handicraft industry, progress in production technology is much slower than that of artificial silk, and costs cannot be reduced at will.

From the above three points, we can see that the quality of artificial silk is currently only worse than that of silk, but because of its suitable weave and affordable price, silk can only sigh with admiration. As for the luster and dyeing of artificial silk, it can be completely comparable to silk. In addition, its quality is improving day by day, becoming more perfect, and adapting to the current world economic crisis, thus providing people with a great need, so we can know that the future of artificial silk is indeed booming and unlimited.

The Standing Committee of the Central Executive Committee, along with Vice Chairman Chiang and other Central Committee members in Beijing, expressed their delight upon hearing that Chairman Hu would be passing through Hong Kong soon. Ju, Ye, and Chen arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning by train and visited Mr. Wang Jingwei, Chairman of the Central Political Council, for a meeting. Three Banks Approve Loans to Money Shops; Repayments Allowed After Year-End Closing; Businesses Begin Year-End Closing Procedures; Money Shops Busy Closing Accounts; Market Collections Gradually Increase

As the year-end closing period for all businesses in the 24th year of the Republic of China approaches, the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications have approved the repayment of loans to money shops after the year-end closing period. Money shops have begun closing their accounts, and collections are gradually increasing. Businesses have begun their year-end closing. Details are as follows:

Money Shops Loans Approved for Delayed Repayment

The Ministry of Finance previously allocated 25 million yuan in financial public bonds for the 24th year to assist money shops, and the Money Shop Supervision Committee was established to manage it. The term has now expired. In addition to the 7 million yuan from commercial banks and the Money Shop Reserve, which have been repaid, the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications have allowed the repayment of the remaining 18 million yuan after the year-end closing period. However, the three banks replied that they could not agree to the request to reduce the annual interest rate of 8%.

Businesses Begin Closing Accounts

As the year-end closing period approaches, businesses are trying to collect money from customers. Merchants from the interior are purchasing goods for the New Year. Money shops are busy closing their accounts every day and extending their internal office hours. They plan to issue lists to all customers on the 15th. The runners of each shop are going to various customers to urge them to return overdrafts. Although the banks' annual closing has passed, they are still very busy because the year-end closing period for all businesses is approaching. Collections of money and silver are gradually increasing.

Land Bureau Writes to Banks and Money Shops; Requests That Real Estate Outside Concessions Not Be Discriminated Against; Should Be Included in Cash Reserve; In Order to Work Together to Reverse the Downturn

The Shanghai Land Bureau believes that when banks and money shops grant cash loans, they only recognize real estate within the concessions as reserve assets and do not give the same treatment to those outside the concessions. Therefore, it sent letters to both the Banking Association and the Money Shop Association to argue for equal treatment. The original letter states: "The Bank Loan Committee has five categories of recognized reserve assets when lending cash. Except for categories B, C, and D, which are not related to real estate, category A lists real estate within the Shanghai International Settlement and the French Concession. Real estate outside the concessions is not included. Although category E states that 'other assets not within the first four categories, which are approved by the Executive Committee, are considered reserve assets,' in reality, it appears to be discriminatory, requiring Executive Committee approval for real estate outside the concessions but not for those within the concessions. The Money Shop Joint Reserve clearly stipulates that real estate within the city with appraised value may be considered reserve assets. However, it is rumored that it is extremely rare for real estate outside the concessions to be recognized as reserve assets. This situation is extremely detrimental to real estate in Shanghai, because the economic and financial source of Shanghai lies in real estate, and most of the real estate is outside the concessions. Discriminating against real estate outside the concessions is equivalent to drying up its financial source. Furthermore, since the Bureau has been conducting land surveys, it has been making great efforts to rectify and divide the maps clearly. During the survey, it invited neighboring land guards to identify the boundaries, and after the survey, it drew sketches and notified the owners to sign and confirm them. The acreage is accurate, and the boundaries are clear. The procedures for exchanging certificates are also very meticulous. The Bureau checks property right documents, checks food based on the certificate, and checks the certificate based on food. It confirms that they match before allowing the exchange of certificates. Once the certificate is exchanged, the Bureau ensures that it maintains the certainty of the land certificate, leaving no room for doubt or concern. Compared to the land within the concessions, its stability and certainty are not only not inferior but even superior. Therefore, in terms of fact, it does not seem appropriate to discriminate against real estate outside the concessions. Also, there are 2 million residents in the city outside the concessions, and the deposits they have in various banks are not small. The guarantee of these deposits should be real estate outside the concessions. Since the banks have obtained a large amount of deposits from residents in the city outside the concessions, they should help the development of real estate in the city outside the concessions. Moreover, the government is making every effort to rescue the declining economy. It is fair to say that it is protecting the interests of banks and money shops. However, the recovery of this economic decline cannot be achieved without the cooperation of the people. The path to cooperation must be based on exploring the origin and determining the priorities. The economic and financial source of this city lies in real estate, so things that hinder the city's real estate should be improved as soon as possible. Currently, banks and money shops in this city treat real estate inside and outside the concessions differently when lending cash, which is deemed necessary to improve. From the perspective of the Ministry of Finance and the Municipal Government, the entire government's strength is used to protect the interests of banks and money shops, but the banks and money shops discriminate against real estate in the city. This situation is unreasonable. At this time of economic depression, only cooperation can help. In addition to sending letters separately, we hereby request that you investigate and revise the cash lending method to include real estate outside the concessions and that you do not discriminate when implementing the method, so that public friendship can be maintained."

Oil Mill Trade Association Asks Ministry for Relief

The Shanghai Oil Mill Trade Association sent a letter to the China General Federation of Industry, which reads: "In reply, we received your letter of December 26 of last year, which opened with a letter from the Ministry of Industry stating, 'Recently, various industries have been experiencing difficulties and have requested relief from the Ministry. The Ministry urgently wants to understand the true situation of the recent actual difficulties and their original requests for various industries.' We hereby forward this to you for your investigation and hope you will forward the results of the discussions by various industry meetings regarding whether there are any recent difficulties and the various industry meetings. The oil mill industry is experiencing difficulties, and the matter is not one-sided. To grasp its importance, it seems that financial blockade, high interest rates, and transportation obstruction and high freight rates are the biggest reasons. We hereby list them in two categories, A and B, and present them to your association in detail. (A) Various industries cannot do without finance as a key element. However, our country currently does not have real industrialists, and for hundreds of years, the business system has been based on credit. Therefore, many people use very little capital to operate very large businesses. This is because they rely on credit loans to circulate funds. Most of our oil mills are suffering from this problem. Although each factory has collected 120,000 to 230,000 yuan in capital, most of it is used to build property and set up machines, so all operating funds must be borrowed, and credit loans are the most important. However, since last summer, the financial sector has suddenly contracted, and the money shops were the first to bear the brunt. They were too busy taking care of themselves to help others. However, what was usually relied upon for circulation cannot be abandoned because of this. However, the difficult situation can be said to have reached its extreme. Interest rates should be fair, but the Shanghai financial sector usually charges an annual interest rate of more than 1% for arrears and pledges, while the interest rate for deposits is only 3 to 4% per month. The difference is too great, and an annual interest rate of more than 1% is unheard of in other countries. (B) The raw materials needed by our industry are mainly soybeans and cottonseed. Soybeans are mainly produced in the three northeastern provinces. There are hundreds of oil mills in that area, and the raw materials are consumed locally. The Japanese government encourages factories to produce, so the cost of the oil cakes produced is relatively low, which allows them to be sold in the interior. Shanghai used to be a sales market for that area. However, after the September 18th Incident, Chinese people were forced by righteous indignation, and in order to block leaks, the factories were successively established. Currently, the soybeans purchased by our industry are mostly produced in Anhui, Shandong, and Henan provinces, followed by Jiangxi and Hubei provinces. However, transporting soybeans from Shangqiu, Henan province, to Shanghai costs 270-280 yuan in national currency for every 20 tons, which is 200 bags, or 400 dan, which is a full train, which is 1.34 yuan per bag. If oil cakes made from them are transported to Guangdong province, then there are Guangdong province tax and additional taxes. With such huge expenses, how can the goods from Shanghai factories compete with the goods from the three northeastern provinces? The same price, they can make a profit, but we cannot even cover the cost. The difficulties are already deep. In addition, the beans from Anhui, Shandong, and Henan provinces are mostly transported by the Longhai and Jinpu Railways, but the railway bureau's vehicles are often lacking, and delays are common. Goods shipped from the place of origin can take as long as one or two months to reach Shanghai. The factory cannot receive them, so there are stoppages and late deliveries. Who is responsible for these unexpected difficulties and various losses? The cottonseed purchased by our industry is mostly produced in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces. Over the years, supply has been insufficient, and work is often interrupted. Although it is known that Shandong, Henan, and Shaanxi provinces are cotton-producing areas, and there must be many cottonseeds, the freight is too high, even exceeding the value of the cottonseeds. Therefore, the goods from that area cannot be transported to Shanghai. In short, industrial production depends on raw materials. Our country is vast and rich in resources, and it can be traded for what is needed. However, transportation is limited and difficult, and freight rates are higher than in any other country. For example, the cost of transporting rice from Siam, Yangon, and Saigon to Shanghai is only 67 cents per bag, but the cost of transporting rice from one province to another in our country is 1.34 yuan per bag. The difference is more than double, which is shocking. The above two items are the recent difficulties of our industry. As for the relief measures for item A, we propose that the Ministry of Industry transfer to the Ministry of Finance, ordering the Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications to quickly accept the mortgage of various industries and goods at the lowest interest rate and lend money to ordinary commercial banks and money shops at the lowest interest rate, and order the banks and money shops to reduce the lending interest as much as possible, so that they can still circulate funds among themselves and provide some relief. Otherwise, it is not just our industry that will be difficult to bear, but the entire industrial and commercial sector of the city will be on the verge of collapse. As for item B, we propose that the Ministry of Industry transfer to the Ministry of Railways, requesting that it quickly reduce the freight rates for various native raw materials and order the car affairs offices of the Longhai and Jinpu Railways to increase vehicles, so that passengers and goods can be transported as soon as they arrive, without hindrance, so that goods can flow freely and reduce costs. Then the future of industry will be hopeful. Therefore, we have to make our case to your consideration, and we ask you to submit it to the Ministry of Industry, approving the requested relief measures and ordering them to be implemented quickly. We are very grateful. Sincerely, Shanghai Oil Mill Trade Association.

Director of Yunnan Construction Department, Zhang Banghan, Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday; Scheduled to Return South by Ship This Afternoon

According to the National News Agency, Zhang Banghan, Director of the Construction Department of Yunnan Province, came to Shanghai and then turned to Beijing last year to attend the Fifth National Congress. After completing his official business, he came to Shanghai to work. Later, as the reorganization of the central government was determined, he stayed in Beijing again to visit President Chiang, asking for instructions on future policies, and met with Xu Mo, Director of Political Affairs of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and exchanged views on the Sino-British Yunnan-Burma border survey. He left Beijing for Shanghai the day before yesterday morning. The reporter met Mr. Zhang at his residence yesterday and asked about the recent situation of construction in Yunnan Province and future facilities. He gave a very detailed explanation. The conversation is divided into the following sections:

Yunnan-Burma Border Survey is Underway

Mr. Zhang first said that regarding the Sino-British Yunnan-Burma border survey, the Chinese members, Liang Yugao and Yin Mingde, appointed by the central government, led the technical personnel to arrive at the end of last year. The meeting place for both parties, Husuan, met several times with the members sent by the British side. At the beginning of this year, they set off to the border between the two countries, re-surveyed according to the past signs, and established boundary pillars, so that this long-standing work that has not been resolved for decades and has caused disputes could be completed before the end of March. If this time is exceeded, the climate there is harsh, and it is difficult for those who have not lived there for a long time to stay. As for the survey to be carried out this time, it is limited to the southern section, and it is expected that there will be no problems. Recently, the British have not made any unusual moves in the Ban Hong and Ban Kuang areas. In fact, the natives in the Ban Long area do not show much goodwill towards the British, and even if there are any unusual moves, it will be difficult to make them submit.

Financial Stability and Monetary Unification

Mr. Zhang continued, "Yunnan Province has been the source of the revolution since the Republic of China. The military expenses required for the past campaigns have been huge, and no money has been taken from the people. Instead, paper money has been issued. Therefore, for the past few years, Yunnan Province has almost become a world of paper money, and the value of the currency has plummeted, and the cost of living has increased again. The provincial government has been working hard to maintain this situation. Until recently, it has gradually become stable. Another 35 million yuan of new Fudian banknotes were issued, and at the same time, all previously issued banknotes of 30 million yuan were converted at a rate of five yuan to one yuan of silver. As for the small amount of cash in Yunnan Province, because it contains insufficient silver content, it should actually be used at a rate of two yuan to one yuan of silver that was previously used in Shanghai. Currently circulating in the market, in addition to the new banknotes of 35 million yuan, there are also old banknotes converted at a rate of five yuan to one yuan, about 6 million yuan, and the cash guarantee reserve has reached more than 30 million yuan. Therefore, in terms of finance, it can be said that it is completely stable, and the provincial government is also making every effort to recover all the old banknotes. Therefore, the future of Yunnan's monetary system is quite promising."

Highway Construction Has Achieved Good Results

As for the construction within the province, there have been good results recently. More than 3,000 kilometers of highways have been completed throughout the province, and more than 2,000 kilometers are being measured and will be completed. However, Yunnan Province has always been known for its poverty, and the annual provincial tax revenue is only more than 8 million yuan. All construction is mostly limited by the economy and cannot be carried out. Those in charge often feel that a clever woman cannot cook without rice, but we must not give up because of this. Even in extremely difficult circumstances, we must try our best to do it with a spirit of hard work. Taking the construction of highways as an example, Yunnan Province has always been known as "no three miles of flat ground." Now that we have this achievement, it should also be a manifestation of hard work. He is currently planning to build a large-scale hydroelectric power generation room in Kunming City and to realize the provincial telephone network, etc. It is also learned that Mr. Zhang is scheduled to take the Empress of Canada this afternoon to Hong Kong and then to Yunnan to handle department affairs.

Northern Navigation Company's Beifu Ran Aground in Anqing; Accident Occurred at 10 a.m. Yesterday; Hired Ships to Unload Cargo to Reduce Load and Tow for Rescue

The Beifu, a ship of the Northern Navigation Company on Consular Road in the French Concession, with a deadweight of 1,975 tons, a length of 262 feet 2 inches, a width of 35 feet 4 inches, a depth of 20 feet 3 inches, a draft of 17 feet, and two decks, built in 1902, was heading to the Yangtze River with coal. Yesterday (the 14th) at 10 a.m., when the ship reached above Wuhu, near Anqing, the river level dropped sharply, causing it to run aground 10 miles below Anqing. The ship was deeply embedded in the shallow sand. The captain repeatedly reversed, but could not move. The river level is expected to continue to fall. It was not until yesterday afternoon that a telegram was sent to Shanghai for help and instructions. The company received a telegram at 6 p.m. yesterday and immediately decided to urgently telegraph the Anqing branch office, ordering it to hire barges nearby to go to the stranded area and unload all the cargo in the Beifu, so as to reduce the draft and float it on the river surface, and then send another ship to tow it for rescue.

First Special Court Tries Opium Cases, Sentences According to Opium Suppression Regulations

The Shanghai First Special District Court, in accordance with the ministry's order, will handle opium cases in accordance with the "Opium Suppression and Drug Prohibition Regulations" promulgated by the Anti-Opium Commissioner. This was originally scheduled to be implemented on the 11th of this month. However, the Public Works Department stated that the police personnel were not yet familiar with the regulations, so by the deadline, all opium cases were still prosecuted by the department based on the "Opium Crime Articles" of the Criminal Law. Guo Yunguan, the president of the First Special Court, now believes that the date of implementation has long been decided and it is impossible to postpone it again. Although the Public Works Department, due to procedural reasons, was unable to immediately use the "Opium Suppression and Drug Prohibition Regulations" for prosecution, the court's trial of these opium cases should not continue to apply the "Opium Crime Articles" that have been explicitly abolished by the government. Therefore, he has ordered the criminal court judges of the court to, from today onwards, sentence all opium cases that have been verified according to the "Opium Suppression and Drug Prohibition Regulations" in order to facilitate opium suppression. Therefore, for the opium cases brought to the court by various police stations of the Public Concession yesterday morning, although the Public Works Department still prosecuted based on the Criminal Law, the presiding judges all declared in court that these types of cases must be dealt with in accordance with the newly promulgated regulations. In order to be cautious in sentencing, the court has also, from yesterday onwards, appointed defense lawyers for opium defendants who have not appointed lawyers to defend them.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Writes to Jianghai Customs to Suspend the Sale of Jadeite Boulders

The case has now been filed for administrative litigation in accordance with the law.

Sale will result in irreparable damage. The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce wrote to the Commissioner of Jianghai Customs yesterday, stating: "On the 13th of this month, we received a letter from merchant Chen Kaiqing, stating that a jadeite boulder that had been taxed and fined by Jianghai Customs was taken back and detained. Subsequently, the customs imposed various penalties, including fines, confiscation, and supplementary taxes. An objection was immediately raised, and the Customs Administration decided to maintain the original decision of the customs, and an administrative lawsuit has been filed. According to the decision, the first penalty was due to underreporting the value of the goods, and the second penalty was due to submitting a forged document. This is completely wrong. The first penalty was due to the mistaken identification of the invoice and tax bill as forged. (The invoice stated the value of the goods as 825 rupees, and the tax bill stated the tax amount as 200 rupees. Calculating based on the low tax rate in that area, it should be 600 rupees, which the customs did not believe and arbitrarily set it as 2,000 rupees.) Therefore, the submission of a forged document is the reason for the first penalty. The second penalty is still for the same reason, which is clearly punishing the same crime twice. The penalty at that time was already inappropriate, and now it is even more unbearable. This case is currently in litigation, but today we received a letter from the customs stating that the fine imposed should be paid immediately. If you want to buy back the jadeite boulder, you must prepare the price and come immediately and pay the supplementary tax, otherwise it will be sold for public benefit. Executing the disposal means that the value of the jadeite boulder can only be determined after it has been cut and polished. It is speculative in nature and is different from ordinary goods. Once it is auctioned, it cannot be restored to its original state. We have already contacted the customs to stop the execution. We are sincerely afraid that we will not be able to obtain approval. We intend to ask your chamber to uphold justice, provide assistance, and request that no arbitrary execution be carried out. We are deeply grateful.

Continued Trial of the Dispute Between the Continental Bank, Two or Three Money Exchanges, and Treasury Bill Contracts

The financial community attaches great importance to this case and many people attended the court to listen.

The judge questioned both parties and advised them to reconcile, and pay the supplementary tax, otherwise it would be sold for public benefit. The execution of the disposal. It must be cut and polished to determine its true value; this is highly speculative, making it different from ordinary goods. Once executed and auctioned, it can never be restored. In addition to asking the customs to suspend the execution, we fear that it will be difficult to gain approval. We respectfully ask your esteemed chamber to uphold justice, provide assistance, and ensure that no arbitrary execution is carried out. We would be eternally grateful." Upon arrival at the chamber, it was noted that Chen Kaiqing had, after the objection was decided, filed an administrative lawsuit according to law to seek final redress. As this case has not been decided by the administrative court, it cannot be considered finalized. If it were to be executed directly, the owner of the goods would suffer irreparable damage. Therefore, Article 9 of the Administrative Litigation Law also stipulates that the original authority may, ex officio or at the request of the plaintiff, suspend the execution. Accordingly, we request that your esteemed commissioner of customs temporarily suspend the execution of this case until it has been adjudicated by the administrative court.

Lilli Motor Company Declares Bankruptcy Yesterday

Unable to withstand soaring gasoline prices and intense competition.

The manager has fled, and workers are gathering to demand back wages. Xin Sheng News Agency reports that Lilli Hekiji Motor Co., Ltd., affected by the economic downturn and facing rising gasoline prices and intense competition, has suffered excessive losses and is unable to continue operating. The company declared bankruptcy yesterday, and the manager has fled. One hundred and fifty drivers, coppersmiths, and workers gathered at the company to jointly demand back wages. Details are as follows:

Reasons for Losses: Lilli Hekiji General Company, located at 329 North Suzhou Road, was established jointly by Li Song General Company and others. It has been in operation for many years. The company had seven telephone stations in the concessions: Songquan, Gude Guang, Fulu, Beikai'er Road, Sapo Sai Road, Jielu, Sichuan Road, and Shanzhong Road. The telephone numbers were "16200" in the concessions and "23232" in the Southern City. The company originally had 80 vehicles, mostly covered wagons. Since being affected by the economic downturn and facing intense competition, the manager and shareholder Li Songquan tried to maintain the company by reducing the taxi fare from two dimes to eight cents. However, this faced opposition and was appealed to the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, which ruled that it could not be implemented.

Temporary Shutdown: Now, with the rising gasoline prices, the company closed three branch stations on Jie Road and Shanzhong Road. It scrapped 20 of the 80 old and dilapidated vehicles and tried to tighten its belt to maintain the status quo. It also offered single deliveries for one yuan, exempting the usual two-dime tip, in an attempt to make a final stand. However, the business continued to be affected by the economic downturn, making it impossible to sustain. The company suddenly announced its closure yesterday. The company's vehicles were parked at the general company on North Suzhou Road and at various branch stations. A public notice reading "Temporarily Closed" was posted at the entrance of the general company.

Workers Demand Back Wages: The company's drivers, coppersmiths, and workers, totaling about 150, gathered at the general company yesterday to inquire about the situation after the company closed. A Xin Sheng News Agency reporter visited the general company yesterday afternoon and learned that the manager, Li Songquan, was still at the company. According to reports, the company owed the workers three months' wages. The reporter also learned from reliable sources that the company's debts were not significant, and the amount owed was roughly the same as the amount it was owed. Therefore, it is said that the company will be formally liquidated.

Altering Lottery Tickets to Claim Rewards, Attempt to Deceive Discovered

Cao Chunsheng Detained Awaiting Sentencing

Cao Chunsheng, a 17-year-old worker at the Meiwen Printing House at 622 Nanjing Road, bought a one-yuan "Overseas" lottery ticket from the Fulai Lottery Shop at 623 Nanjing Road, across from the printing house, for the 18th Aviation Highway Construction Lottery. The last digit of the lottery number Cao bought was the same as the last digit of the first prize number. According to the rules, he could redeem a one-yuan prize. However, Cao had a fanciful idea and found a discarded lottery ticket. He cut off the seven Chinese and Western characters in the number and pasted them onto the "Hundred Changes Four" characters on the number of the lottery ticket he bought, changing it to 234775, which happened to be the same as the sixth prize number drawn in this period. At 11:00 AM on the 13th, Cao held the lottery ticket and redeemed the 10-yuan sixth prize at the Dachangcheng Tobacco and Paper Shop, which also sold aviation tickets, at 120 Xin Kaihe Road, Huangpu Beach, French Concession. He was discovered by Gao Zengshi, the shop owner from Ningbo, who immediately called Detective Yao Zhupo and a patrol officer to arrest Cao. Cao was detained and taken to the police station along with the altered lottery ticket. Yesterday morning, Cao was detained and taken to the police station along with the altered lottery ticket. Yesterday, the court stated the facts of the case, stating that the defendant was detained for altering valuable securities with the intention of defrauding money. The police station still needs to conduct a detailed investigation and requested a one-week extension to investigate the case. Then, Detective Yao Zhupo reported the circumstances of the arrest and submitted the altered lottery ticket to the court. According to the witness Gao Zengsai's statement, the defendant fraudulently redeemed the reward with the altered ticket. Cao Chunsheng admitted to cutting and pasting the ticket. After verifying the confession, Judge Wang Gangxu ordered that the trial be rescheduled to 21st. The defendant was returned to custody.

Two Assassins Fled the Scene

Seriously Injured in Vital Areas

Lu was caught off guard and immediately fell to the ground in pain, lying in a pool of blood. By the time family members and beat police arrived after hearing the sound, the perpetrators had already fled far away. They immediately reported the incident to the Xibaoxing Road branch police station, which dispatched police to search for the perpetrators.
