Shen Bao Local Supplement

Commentary

Catching the Book Thief

— Jia Wei

I happened to visit a semi-public library that has a sign saying "Non-members or those without an annual reading certificate worth one yuan are not allowed to enter," and I saw a notice about "catching the book thief."

According to the notice: recently, some "immoral person" tore out a part of an English "Modern Historical Materials" magazine. Following that, some "similar" people took away English magazines such as "Asia" and "Middle School Students," which were "for public reading," from the bookshelves. Therefore, readers are asked to pay attention and help catch this "clever thief."

Damn it, our vast society is constantly producing these "scum." Previously, there were university students who became thieves, defrauded people of their money, became robbers... doing things that "铤而走险 (risk their lives)," and now there are "scholars" who take one or two magazines from public places, committing small thefts of "顺手牵羊 (taking something easily)." "Propriety, justice, integrity, and a sense of shame" have been "lost completely." Truly, "the world is deteriorating, and people's hearts are not as good as before"—our moralistic gentlemen will "exclaim with emotion"!

I remember reading Lu Xun's "Kong Yiji" before—a person known for habitually stealing books—who said: "Stealing books doesn't count as theft... Stealing books... It's a scholar's business, how can it be considered stealing?..."

This is just Mr. "Kong Yiji's" sophistry, right? But he still says "君子固窃 (a gentleman steals as a matter of course)," "何者 (why)?" and other such "defending the Way" nonsense.

Here, we are certainly not going to compare these "stealing books" "thieves" who "take advantage of" the library with Mr. "Kong Yiji," who is famous for stealing books. But from this, we can better understand one side of our society: the extent to which the lives of ordinary "book-reading people" have become impoverished, and how serious the problem has become for the prospects of ordinary young "intellectuals."

However, no one can deny that today, with the entire social economy collapsing and the countryside bankrupt, cities depressed, markets withering, and all industries declining, the general working class is being abandoned by a small group of special people to struggle and compete on the line of hunger and death. The middle class of our society—small property owners—will inevitably and continuously become impoverished and decline... and our "book-reading people" and "intellectuals" will follow suit and become a problem!

Therefore, perhaps we can believe that the "book thief" mentioned above who tore out a part of a magazine and took away the entire magazine also has the same meaning as when "Kong Yiji" was ridiculed for his "sophistry": "Stealing books doesn't count as theft; stealing books, it's a scholar's business..." However, we can also believe that perhaps these "pests" will not be like "Kong Yiji," who "stole" one or two magazines worth a few mao to sell and buy wine to drink, right? But things seem to be similar. Thinking about the crowded "reader" who tore and "stole" a part of the English magazine, is he planning to translate it and sell it to solve his hunger?

Finally, we want to declare that we are not here to defend or protect these "book thieves." For these "immoral" and "without propriety, justice, integrity, and a sense of shame" "pests" and "scum," we should "pay attention together and help catch them." However, the matter must be clarified: is this just a matter of "stealing"!

Seagull

— Laborious Mind

—The Story of Sea Travel—

After the cargo ship passed the Lion's Gate, everyone could steal a little free time.

Third Uncle sat on the rudder handle with his buttocks, slowly filling the foot-long pipe with a bowl of Lao Nongfu brand tobacco, striking a match, and pressing the tobacco on the pipe with his thumb. After a while, the fire approached the tobacco, and he began to suck on it with a "hulu hulu" sound. After a dense cloud of smoke was exhaled from his mouth, he began to nag us:

"Hoist the sail, did you forget? Useless, you bunch of Guangya Lane goods!"

We were startled and stood up, blindly hoisting the mast. Lao Gui quickly and nimbly grabbed and unfurled the sail. Lao Qi and I rushed to first erect the mast, hang the sail, and slowly unfurl it. We didn't make a sound, nor did we sing "yo ai yo" as usual while working. We were used to Third Uncle's temper. If you didn't argue with him and listened to him and worked smoothly, you could avoid hearing a lot of nagging.

This time, we had a chance to chat.

We sat on the cargo on the bow of the ship. The three of us, even Fifth Uncle, walked up from the stern, leaving Third Uncle alone to smoke his pipe—

"Damn it, we have to work even during the New Year, will we really have to work until New Year's Eve?"

Lao Qi, this guy with the worst temper, anything put in his stomach would turn into dynamite and explode. He loved to complain about himself, but he never really did what he said he would do. Fifth Uncle often ridiculed him for this.

"Lao Qi, you're losing your temper again! Who told you to do it? Why don't you go back and enjoy yourself—don't you want your old man to be reborn to serve you?"

"Old man, opening your mouth with old man, closing your mouth with old man, you are the son of a whore."

"You're really a savage, unreasonable, and no one is arguing with you!"

"Who is arguing with you? If you want to fight, fight in the Dragon King's palace!"

When two crickets meet, they often fight. We all resented the two of them, even during this free time, they mixed it up with吵呀闹地 (fighting and making noise), which was damn boring. Lao Gui lay diagonally, his eyes half-closed, with a bit of impatience:

"Dead cow! If you want to fight or make noise, why don't you go into the water! People are worrying about not being able to spend this free time peacefully, but you look like you have energy but nowhere to expend it."

Really, once we left the mouth of Lion's Gate, we could think about having a good time. There was no wind or waves here. The downstream boat just happened to be carried by the wind and water, without having to exert any effort.

The water surface was very calm. In the distance, there were occasionally one or two jumping fish, suddenly jumping up, opening a small hole in the water, the splash of water piercing very high. Following that, a small circle of water chased a large circle of water, the circles getting bigger and bigger, farther and farther. In the end, after taking a bath in the sun, reflecting the subtle ripples, it slowly disappeared.

Lao Gui sighed. I saw him staring at the flight of three or four seagulls, his heart seeming to be troubled by something, restless. I approached him and gently patted him:

"Lao Gui, what's so good about seagulls?"

He jumped up, raised his head as if someone had discovered a secret, looked at me, then lowered it again.

"Damn it! Seagulls are free. We have to work even during the New Year, not even as good as seagulls. It's not that Lao Qi has a bad temper, as long as there is a way to survive, 野仔 (even a wild child) would run away…"

Lao Qi's complaints插过 (interrupted) again. Lao Gui sneered. Fifth Uncle said:

"What's wrong with you again? Seagulls are free? Aren't they just doing it for food? You complain about having to work during the New Year? You're really an ungrateful person. I'd like to see you when you don't have anything to eat…"

"Ancestors for eighteen generations, you have to go against me, didn't I owe you money in my previous life!"

"What are you arguing about?" Lao Gui said with a bit of bitterness, "骂来骂去 (scolding each other) are all our own people, what's the point!" Lao Gui hadn't finished speaking when a very shrill "chi" sound rang out, and then we saw a pair of seagulls with broken feathers falling into the water. At first, it was still desperately holding its wings in the water, but when it couldn't hold on anymore, it was so weakly immersed in the water. Its body was surrounded by fish, and every now and then another pair of seagulls flew down, pecking a piece of meat from its body, and flying back.

We sighed and lowered our heads. Lao Gui stood up instead, exercising his arms, but eventually collapsed on the cargo again.

Winter Gloom

— Zhuang Ruiyuan

Winter is the season of autumn's nostalgia and spring's anticipation.

Without sunshine, without rain or snow, but ice destroys the vitality of grass and trees, condenses on the roof, on the branches, in the ditches, clings to nests without birds, and covers roads without pedestrians, there are often such days in winter.

On these days, I have no joy, no sorrow, my emotions belong to the winter gloom, paler than a winter morning. Even when covered in sunshine, drenched in rain and snow, I only have the feeling of light smoke. And I like to savor the thin dreams of autumn and the magnificent aspirations of spring.

Therefore, it is easy to feel lonely on gloomy winter days!

The loneliness in the room is more terrifying than the cold outside the house, and more so than the melancholy on the street and the harshness of the countryside.

In the morning, winter stands forlornly at my window, so there is a surge of the sea between the window sill, the window screen, and the curtains. The ice flowers clinging to the glass panes, and the ice columns hanging down, only add to the strangeness for me. I love to rest under the wall blocking the north wind because in the December sun, the bronze-golden old robe, the dust-covered old hat, and the opened book mean a suitable adjustment to loneliness.

I also like to wander the streets, from calmness to hustle and bustle, and from hustle and bustle to calmness, listening to the noisy sounds of the city, and watching my own steps. (Even on the cold winter streets, I have a lazy pace.) So, the one walking in the piles of run-down houses is me; the one looking at the woman selling roasted sweet potatoes at the bridgehead is me; the one looking for traces of children's spinning tops in the open space is me. And I often say to myself: how unbearable it would be to live in a cold room, living a bland and tasteless life.

And walking in the countryside is also a joy. I shrink my neck into my collar, put my hands in my pockets, and half-close my eyelids to resist the sharp wind of the wilderness. Winter has an even more ridiculous face. The weeds of autumn cannot withstand a night of狂风 (gale), ice, and frost, bending down and lying on the ground; the trees of winter have leafless branches that forcefully pierce into the low-pressure sky, which makes me think of the direction of the wild geese, and all the more secretly laugh at the rugged winter gloom.

But these are just casual hobbies. I have no bias against winter, neither hatred nor fondness. It's just in the淡白 (pale) emotions that I warm thin dreams and magnificent aspirations.

On gloomy winter days, I abhor loneliness more than I abhor the bitter cold.

Blue Overcoat

— Hua Mu

In the playground, Teacher Yang's silver whistle rang. A group of elementary school students, like a flock of little lambs, came running and jumping. They finally formed a square tofu-like formation. Teacher Yang, standing in front, blew the whistle again, and the little eyes of a flock of little lambs all looked over towards the teacher.

"Listen up, now prepare to go to the city to visit the exhibition. I told you yesterday that anyone who doesn't wear a blue overcoat will stay at school. Everyone look at yourselves, and anyone who doesn't wear a blue overcoat should automatically step out."

As soon as Teacher Yang finished speaking, a buzzing sound rose from the flock of little lambs, and their black little heads kept leaning forward and backward, and the formation became chaotic. Several multicolored guys quietly retreated from the center to a corner of the playground, their small eyes looking at the classmates who remained in the playground as if they had been wronged. Little Mao A-san jumped up and down happily, flipping over and pushing Ma Dacheng in the back row.

"You don't have a blue overcoat!" Ma Dacheng glared at Little Mao fiercely, ignoring her.

Teacher Yang's whistle rang again, and his face was obviously not as natural as before.

"Listen up! Haven't I often told you that a good student should be obedient and follow the rules? Ma Dacheng—why don't you step out?"

The black little heads in front all turned around again. Ma Dacheng's little face immediately turned as red as if it had been painted with a

Page 20

layer of rouge. But she said very calmly.

"I want to go too." Her tone seemed very stubborn and crisp. The playground suddenly became quiet. Teacher Yang's face showed an even more unnatural color. He thought to himself, this child is too naughty, so he said:

"You want to go too? Then why don't you wear a blue overcoat?"

"My mom said that a black overcoat is the same, and I didn't make a blue overcoat." The playground burst into laughter.

"You know that's not true, who told your mom not to make one for you? Looking like you, you can't even wear an overcoat properly. The outside is not like the school, you'll be laughed at, you know that! Quick, quick, step out for me!" Teacher Yang walked over from the front and pushed Ma Dacheng out with one hand. Ma Dacheng burst into tears:

"My mom said that a black overcoat is the same, and I didn't make a blue overcoat, wuwu…"

The little lambs in the playground thought it was extremely funny and laughed again with a "poof" sound.

Teacher Yang walked back to the front as if nothing had happened, blew the whistle again, and shouted:

"Attention—at ease, original formation, turn left. March!"

The playground was quiet and寂寂 (silent), leaving behind a cloud of yellow dust…

Movies

The Director of "Wild Geese Descending on the Sandy Beach"

Ma Xubang—the director of "Wild Geese Descending on the Sandy Beach," has been working hard for more than ten years, from the early days of Chinese cinema to the present, taking on various jobs, gaining a lot of experience, trying various creations, and achieving a lot of success.

He has a special personality, a special style, values emotion, loves beauty, seeks and researches, has the vigor of youth, the demeanor of a humble gentleman, and an attitude of not being ashamed to ask those below him.

Because of this, you can further understand that he is serious, strong, and creative. He uses these spirits to engage in work and to engage in everything.

You can recognize from his works that he has a beautiful and affectionate appearance, with a great and calm ambition hidden in his heart.

He still completed this "Wild Geese Descending on the Sandy Beach" with the spirit of being as still as a virgin and as quick as a rabbit. In his spare time from work, he can relax and chat with you about anything, and he talks very enthusiastically. When he is working, even a tiny detail will concentrate all his energy, and he will not let go in the slightest.

You can recognize this outstanding artist from his works.

Recent News from the Shanghai Drama and Film Research Institute

The Shanghai Drama and Film Research Institute, located in the Park Square on Jiangwan Road, Shanghai, has been very active since the New Year of 1936. Recently, in addition to attending classes for four hours every day and stepping up rehearsals of basic movements, the institute is also actively preparing for its first drama performance. It is said that it has now selected the play "The First Flag of Europe," which contains profound and sharp anti-imperialist significance, and "Human World," a famous expressionist play of the latest form that has never been seen on the Chinese stage. Both plays are currently being translated. As soon as the script is translated, rehearsals will begin immediately. At the same time, because the first class of the institute has been open for more than two months, there is an endless stream of people requesting to enter the institute. Therefore, the second recruitment is now being held. Detailed recruitment information can be obtained by sending a letter with two cents postage attached.

The Tragedy of "Brothers"

In Hu Die's "Brothers," she and Gao Zhanfei fall in love and marry, giving birth to a son named Xianglin (played by Liang Kaiyuan). Soon, Gao Zhanfei marries Zhu Qiuhen and abandons her. In order to make a living, Hu Die throws away her son and finally marries Xiao Ying. The following year, she also gives birth to a child named Dexin (played by Shen Junchi).

Seven years later, this couple, because of their poor health, go to the seaside in Zha Pu for recuperation. Dexin is very interested in the shells on the beach. On the beach, he meets a child who is one year older than him. Because of the child's mother's story, Hu Die knows that this child is Xianglin, the son she had with Gao Zhanfei, but she doesn't dare to admit that he is her child, so she has to secretly caress Xianglin. Dexin and Xianglin are really too close. They go to the beach every day when the tide recedes to pick up shells. One day, Dexin doesn't know the danger and runs off alone. It happens to be when the tide is rising. By the time Xianglin arrives and discovers the danger, the tide has covered the beach. He knows that it is too late to call someone to save him, so he bravely jumps into the water, struggling with Dexin in the tide. However, his strength is ultimately insufficient. By the time others rescue them, they have already stopped breathing. Hu Die falls on their bodies, crying her heart out. She has been stimulated by being abandoned, and now she has lost two beloved sons. What a great tragedy!

Shen Bao Local Supplement Automobile Special Issue

Automobile Using Wood Instead of Oil

— Mingde

Recently read a German transportation magazine. Saw a record of German automobiles using wood instead of oil. Translated it below. For the reference of those who study automobile fuel.

Using solid fuel, such as wood, such as coal, to replace liquid fuel, such as automobiles, gasoline, to power factories and vehicle engines, French people had already tried and succeeded after the European War. The best structure of the French gasification-for-oil furnace is the one invented by Mr. Imbert. Now almost all French military vehicles have been converted to use Imbert gasification furnaces instead of gasoline.

The German side has also undergone several tests. First, coal gasification furnaces were built and installed in automobiles, but the firebricks built in the coal gasification furnaces were easily detached due to the vibration of the vehicles during operation, and could not be used. Later, the Imbert wood gasification furnace was used instead, and the results were very good. Compared with using oil, about 92% of the cost can be saved.

The Imbert wood gasification furnace can be divided into four main parts: the gasification furnace body, the condenser filter, the fan, and the air pipe. The entire furnace weighs about 100 to 150 kilograms. The gasification furnace body is made of iron plates and is shaped like a round tube. It is divided into inner and outer layers, about 1.5 meters high and 0.5 meters in diameter. There are no furnace firebricks and water jackets for cooling inside. There are many holes in the lower part of the furnace body. Some of the holes have covers that can be opened and closed to check the amount of charcoal stored in the furnace. Other parts of the holes have tongues that open and close inward. The charcoal is ignited through these holes when starting a fire. After the fire is lit, the air required for gasification in the furnace also flows in through these holes. However, when the gas in the furnace flows outward, the tongues will close automatically. In addition, there is also an ash discharge hole in the lower part. There is a cover on the upper part of the furnace body. After the cover is opened, firewood can be loaded. (Any kind of large wood chips can be used, but they must not be longer than 8 centimeters.) After the cover on the furnace is closed, the burning igniter is inserted through the ignition hole. The fan is turned on at the same time, and the charcoal in the furnace will burn. However, because there is too little air, it will not burn completely, and gas will be generated. After burning for about three or four minutes, the gas generated in the furnace is enough to start the engine. Then, the gas in the furnace passes through the air pipe to the condenser filter first, and the water and ash contained in the gas are condensed and retained in the condenser filter. This clean and cooled gas then passes through the air pipe fan to the air door. Here, it is mixed with the air flowing in from the outside to become gas suitable for the engine. It enters the汽缺 through the engine's intake valve. After the engine starts, the fan can be stopped. After that, the airflow in the furnace is completely drawn by the engine. If the automobile engine is stopped for about 15 minutes, the gas in the furnace can still start the engine. However, if the engine is stopped for too long, the fan must be used to restart the fire. The fan can be operated manually. If you want to eliminate the fan, there are two methods: Store a part of the gas generated in the furnace in another box. When starting the engine, use this stored gas. Initially use the automobile to start the engine.

The gas generated by the Imbert gasification furnace generates a burst pressure of 20 kilograms per cubic centimeter in the engine, which is about 10 kilograms smaller than gasoline per cubic centimeter. The burning rate in the汽缺 is also lower. Therefore, the engine runs very quietly, and it can reduce the engine's ignition problems in summer. As for fuel consumption, each time about 100 kilograms of firewood can be loaded into the furnace, which can travel 70 to 90 kilometers. Compared with gasoline, 2.2 kilograms of firewood can replace 1 kilogram of gasoline, so the cost is very economical.

Overview of American Automobile Sales at the End of the Year

— Lingyun

1935 has ended. 1936 has just begun. The American automobile manufacturing industry is at its most critical juncture at this time. Each car factory is trying its best to manufacture new cars to meet the needs of all parties. On the customer side, because the 1936 model new cars have already been released, they have decided which car they want to buy at this time. Orders are sent from the hands of dealers to the factory like snowflakes. According to news from Detroit, the total number of cars manufactured by each factory in the two months of November and December at the end of 1935 was about 700,000. This number should not be underestimated. Of course, Ford and Chevrolet are still the main producers among the factories. Their products are at the top. The weekly output is about 90,000 vehicles. People in the automobile industry expect that if nothing unexpected happens and the sales of automobiles are affected, then the manufacturing plans of each factory will be carried out completely according to the predetermined plan. The factory's output and sales are trending in the same direction. The future can be said to be good. In short, the factory's shipments are entirely based on sales. It is not difficult to adjust temporarily if there are changes in the market.

Since the autumn automobile exhibition, the automobile industry in Detroit has been showing a lively atmosphere. This is undeniable. The advantage that salesmen took in this exhibition was that they could immediately promise customers to deliver new cars quickly. Unlike when the exhibition was held in the first month of the year, customers wanted the goods, but the factory could not deliver them for a long time, which made people very impatient. Salesmen also discovered at the new car exhibition last autumn that most customers were prepared with cash and wanted to take their favorite new cars home immediately. Because of the strong sales of cars, each factory is working day and night, trying its best to rush production. The employment index in Detroit has also risen accordingly, and is at its highest level similar to September in 1933.

We only need to look at the weekly output of each factory to know the tense atmosphere in Detroit. The weekly output of each factory is as follows: Ford 25,000 vehicles, Chevrolet 25,000 vehicles, Plymouth 9,000 vehicles, Dodge 7,500 vehicles, Pontiac 6,000 vehicles, Walters Marmobile 5,000 vehicles, Buick 4,500 vehicles, Hudson Terraplane 3,500 vehicles, Packard 2,000 vehicles, Nash Lafiayette 1,350 vehicles, Studebaker 1,000 vehicles. There are many other factories that manufacture less than 1,000 vehicles per week. The largest comparative output among various vehicles is Buick, Packard, Dodge, Pontiac, Walters Marmobile, and Nash cars, which are priced around 1,000 US dollars. The good sales of these cars show that the sales of slightly higher-priced cars are good. This situation is completely different from 1931, 1932, 1933, and 1934. Looking at the end of 1935, Ford, General Motors, and Chrysler made the most profits. However, in general people's minds, 1936 is a very good year for several independent factories. The recent sales conferences held in New York and Chicago have clearly shown that the small factories are working hard to strive for their business.

Studebaker held an aggressive sales plan in December. According to George, the deputy sales manager, the total output in December could reach 10,000 vehicles. The output of the company's new Los Angeles factory could increase by 1,000 vehicles. Nash has also set a specific plan for the sales of 1936 model new cars. The most important thing is to use grand advertising sales. It is estimated that the sales in 1936 will increase by 75%. The output of Nash and Lafiayette in 1935 was about 75,000 vehicles. After the planned increase in output, the total number will be 130,000 vehicles.

The sales of Huppermobile in 1935 have shown a significant increase compared to the past three years. In the past ten months, the company encountered legal disputes. Everything has now been resolved. The sales department has also been reorganized, and McDonald has been appointed as the director. Graham-Paige's 1936 sales plan focuses on new-style low-priced cars with supercharged models. Domestic and overseas sales are being vigorously promoted. This plan coincides with the company's deputy manager Graham's promotion of the world market. Hudson estimates that its output will reach 33,500 vehicles by January 1 of this year. This is much more than the 25,000 vehicles planned earlier. According to Tralsher, the deputy manager of the sales department, the retail sales at the New York exhibition have broken the record of the past five years, and have increased by two and a half times compared to the previous year.

The German Opel Automobile Factory is commemorating the grand event of the 1936 Summer Olympics, which will be held in Berlin. The 1936 Model Huppermobile New Car

— Fu

Will Be Exhibited in Shanghai Soon

The 1936 model six-cylinder and eight-cylinder Huppermobile new cars are equipped with newly designed and transformed car bodies and a unique superior transmission that allows for carefree driving and operation. Therefore, their effectiveness is grand and outstanding, and their styles are extremely beautiful and moving. According to Mr. Gu Denan, the sales director of the local Huppermobile dealer, the Kangtai Automobile Company, this new car will be publicly displayed at the latest by the end of this month to meet with the people of Shanghai. Mr. Gu is currently actively arranging to hold the first exhibition of the new car in the sample room at 627 Foch Road within the last week of this month.

Huppermobile products have always been famous in the world for their beautiful styles. Now, the new cars are even more beautiful and spectacular. The new cars are divided into two major groups. Their graceful posture is not only pleasing to the eye and fascinating, but also reduces air resistance to the lowest possible limit. The interior is also more spacious and comfortable. The weight and passengers have been redistributed as much as possible. Therefore, it is extremely comfortable to be in them. In addition, what is even more commendable is that Huppermobile, in addition to being famous in the world for its absolute reliability and durability for twenty-eight years, has countless mechanical engineering features in terms of design and construction. These advantages are only available in vehicles with twice the price. Now, the new Huppermobile car has everything, which is even more commendable.

British-Made Eight-Wheel Truck

— Yingdai

—Very Economical Freight—

The British Overseas Transport Advisory Committee has been studying an economical transportation method for several years to remedy the higher freight rates of railway transportation. This transportation method can reduce costs on the one hand, and can avoid increasing road maintenance costs on the other hand. The purpose is nothing more than to develop the transshipment business in the colonies. The first group of transport vehicles was ordered by the Gold Coast government in 1933 to try out some vehicles first. A second group was ordered again the following year, including an eight-wheel tractor. All eight wheels can be turned and carry a load of three tons, and two eight-wheel trailers, each carrying a load of six tons. Therefore, fifteen tons of goods can be loaded on twenty-four light pneumatic tires. The pressure on the ground is much less per square inch than a normal thirty CW seven freight truck. Because of the increased number of wheels, the pressure exerted on the ground by trucks traveling overseas is the lightest with this type of vehicle. All axles are completely independent and direct-acting to reduce the vibration of the vehicle when traveling on the road. As for the trailer, four wheels are in a group, and the two groups of wheels are installed together. Even when they are completely locked, they will not leave the vehicle's ruts.

The second group of vehicles is similar to each other in terms of manufacturing, and the trailer was manufactured by the United Car Factory in accordance with all the instructions given by the Advisory Committee. It uses a diesel engine instead of a car engine. Only the first and fourth wheels can slide, which can reduce a lot of costs in terms of manufacturing and maintenance. The load is the same as the first group, which is also fifteen tons, but if it is on a flat road, the trailer can be increased to eight tons, and the tractor can be increased to four tons. Therefore, three trucks can carry 20 tons of goods. During the trial period, it initially traveled 9,937 miles in central Australia, followed by 550 miles in the south. It went to Olspin in the north, and then to Balden, which is the end of the North Australian Railway. In addition, it has been to several locations. In short, the results of the trial are very satisfactory in everything, and the land that the trial has passed is
